aakhirkaar kareeb 30 ghante ke baad mumbai kii lifline main jaan aa hi gai
 More than a thousand striking motorman declared to end their strike
 shaayad sarkaar kii sakhti or sarkaar kii apil donon ne mumbai kii lifline ko patari par laane main ahm bhoomika adaa kii lekin in 30 ghanton main mumbai kii raftaar par brake laga rahaa
 In view of the difficulties of about 70 lakh passengers, the Maharashtra government also had to come into action
 rajya sarkaar ko mumbai ke hadataali motorman par esma ko lagu karnaa hi padaa
 More than 150 motormans were arrested in Mumbai
 sarkaar ne apane tevar sakht kar liye the
 Perhaps the result of this is that the striking motorman of Mumbai announced to withdraw their strike before 5 o'clock in the evening
 idhar mumbai se saadhe 15 sau kilometre dur dilli main sansad main hadtaal ko lekar hangaame kii gunj sunai di or kahana galat nahin hoga ki motorman kii hadtaal khatm hone main iskaa bhi asar rahaa
 Apart from Shiv Sena and BJP, leaders of other parties also started pressuring the government regarding the strike
 udhar khud mumbai main bhi hadtaal ko khatm karaane ke liye emenes pramukh raaj thakare ne motorman ko shaam tak kaam par lautne kii chetavanee di thi
 It is possible that motormen may have been forced to withdraw the movement due to the threat of Raj Thackeray and the uproar of MNS activists
 emenes kii virdohi shivasena bhi shuru se hadtaal ke virodh main utar ai thi
 It is clear that both the government's strictness and the government's appeal played a role in ending the motorman strike
 esma yaa phir baatcheet se, ummid samasya ke samaadhaan kii thi or hua bhi bilkul vaisaa hi
 Shahrukh's daughter Suhana Khan has turned 16 in June 2016
 unki khubsuurati ko dekhakar aap tarif kiye bagaiyr nahin rah paaenge
 a glimpse of this was seen at the New Year party, whose pictures were also shared by Suhana on her Instagram account
 shahrukh khan ke janmdin par jabasuhanane laal rang kii dress pahani to logon kii tarif rukne kaa naam hi nahin le rahe the
 Now seeing the way in which Suhana has taken pictures on New Year, it seems that Kisuhana has now grown up
 
 
 suhanane apane best frends ke saath mumbai ke ek nite club main new year celibratt kiya
 Sanjay Kapoor's daughter Shanaya, Chunky Pandey's daughter Ananya and Dine Pandey's son Ahan were also with him at the party
 is party mensuhanaki puri gang ne blike and white kapade pahane the
 Please tell that Shahrukh's daughter Suhana, Anil Kapoor's niece Shanaya Kapoor and Chunky Pandey's daughter Ananya are very good friends
 teenon ko aksar parties main saath dekha jaataa he
 JIPMER MBBS 2019: JIPMER exam conducted by Jawaharlal Institute of Postgraduate Medical Education and Research is on 2 June
 is saal kul 1,84,272 candidats ne pariksha ke liye aavedan kiya tha
 Of these, 94,073 students will appear in the morning shift and 90,199 students in the evening shift
 yah pariksha 280 centres main yojit kii jaaegi
 The results of the examination will be released on or before 21 June
 pariksha ke baad 26 june se 28 june tak first round counselling hogi
 There will be second round counseling on 24 July, third round counseling on 21 August and final round counseling on 26 September
 subject-viz marks- physics - 60- chemistry - 60- biology - 60- english language and comprihension - 10- logical and quantetitive rijning - 10JIPMER MBBS pariksha main safal candidats puducheri or karaikal ke 200 sits par daakhila praapt kar sakate hai
 This course is of four years and 6 months
 saath hi ek saal kaa compalsri rotetary internship bhi he
 Anna Hazare was taking vows to fight corruption in association with Baba Ramdev on Friday, but now his team is saying that there will be no joint movement with him
 team anna ne baithak ke baad kaha ki ramdev ke saath saajha andolan nahin hoga
 On the other hand, Ramdev said that he would come to a stage if needed
 ramdev ne kaha ki chaahe vah team anna kaa andolan ho yaa unka donon se logon main jaagrukta aegi
 Ramdev said that our fight is against corruption
 isse pehle, team anna kii kor cameti kii baithak main ravivaar ko us vakt vivaad paidaa ho gaya jab ek sadsy ko kathith rup se apane mobile phone par kaarywahi record kar use baahar prasaarit karte paaya gaya or jiske baad use baithak se baahar chale jane ko kaha gaya
 Team Anna was meeting in Noida adjacent to Delhi to discuss the upcoming strategy and alliances, including alliances with yoga guru Baba Ramdev
 is dauraan team ke sadsy mufti shamoon kaasmi ko kathith rup se kaarywahi kii recordig karte paaya gaya
 Talking to reporters after the meeting, Team Anna member Prashant Bhushan said that when Kasmi was asked about the recordings, she denied having any information about it
 bhushan ke mutabik kaasmi ne kaha ki recording sanyogvash he
 Bhushan told reporters, "he got angry when we asked him to admit his mistake
 anna hajaare ne bhi unase sanyam rakhane kii apil kii lekin vah aape se baahar ho gaye
 We have come to know that he is talking stupid things outside
 " Bhushan said that Kasami was asked to leave the meeting for a while
 team anna ke duusare pramukh sadsy arvind kejariwal ne kaha ki swami agnivesh kii tarah kaasmi ko range-haath pakadaa gaya
 Last year, during the Anna Hazare hunger strike at Delhi's Ramlila Maidan, the decisions of the team meeting were conveyed to the ministers of the Swami government
 kejariwal ne kaha, "swami agnivesh kii tarah kaasmi range-haath pakade gaye hai
 "team Anna member Shazia Ilmi also targeted Kasami
 ilmi ne kaha ki team ne yah kehete hue kaasmi kaa virodh kiya, "aap kor cameti ke sadsy hai
 Discussion about the strategy going on is going on and you are recording and broadcasting the conversation outside
 iske aage, aap daawa kar rahe hai ki aap aisa isliye kar rahe hai kyonki aap ek muslim hai? yah atyant aniatik baat he or iske liye apane dharm ko dhaal bananaa or bhi buree cheez he

 It is noteworthy that before the second phase of the budget session of Parliament, this meeting of Team Anna was focused on strengthening its strategy for an effective Lokpal Bill
 bajet satr kaa doosraa charan mangalvaar se shuru ho rahaa he
